*16:59 2016/02/24
*this is an example of a simple regex script for TAHelper on VNR
*originally it was made based on ATLAS V14 (+TA) behaviour
*Update: the script adapting LEC behaviour now, so might not work on ATLAS or other translation engine
*basically only for conversation text, so might not work on RPG or games with lots of "status" thing..
*
*
*
*
*
*topmost line = top priority
*sometimes to make it work properly, it should be sorted by characterset
*hiragana order : ぁあぃいぅうぇえぉおかがきぎくぐけげこごさざしじすずせぜそぞただちぢっつづてでとどなにぬねのはばぱひびぴふぶぷへべぺほぼぽまみむめもゃやゅゆょよらりるれろゎわゐゑをん
*katakana order : ァアィイゥウェエォオカガキギクグケゲコゴサザシジスズセゼソゾタダチヂッツヅテデトドナニヌネノハバパヒビピフブプヘベペホボポマミムメモャヤュユョヨラリルレロヮワヰヱヲンヴヵヶ
*symbols order : 、。，．・：；？！゛゜´｀¨＾￣＿ヽヾゝゞー―‐～…‥‘’“”（）［］｛｝〈〉《》「」『』【】
*kanji start-end : 一-龠 (not really sure...)
*numbers : [0-9] (latin digit), [０-９] (fullwidth digit), [一二三四五六七八九十]
*u-verb list : すくぐぶつむるぬう
*-te form conj list : ([っせべげけめねれて来きしくういえ]|[さわばがかまならあた][れせ]|しえ|なく|まし|[あえ来こ](られ|させ)|あっ)(て)
*-te form list 2 : (([一-龠])([しい]て|[いん]で))
*conditional conj list : ([せえべげけめねれて]|なら|であれ|[あうけくす来]れ)(ば) and なら (unsafe)
*(adj) : ([いさしなたらろつばこ]い)
*(obj-prt) : をがにへとでのはも,から,より,まで
*verb ended with る (not ru-verb) : [あいうえおか-ぢつ-もやゆよら-りれろわ]
*if some characters not work/ignored (ex : “), use TA's substitution instead
*character specific hex code:
*to search specific character, use \x followed by hex code (ex: \x5B )
*"[" = 5B
*"]" = 5D
*"{" = 7B
*"}" = 7D
*"\" = 5C or just use \\
*"|" = 7C
*"?" = 21
*"!" = 3F
*"^" = 5E
*
*
*What this script do :
*1. Cleaning text
*2. Converting various dialects into normal form
*
*What's hard to-do :
*1. Slurism (intonation based text)
*2. Full hiragana or katakana text
*3. Clause (quoted text, mixed clauses without conjuctions or particles, or connected by って)
*4. 何, どう etc (how, how many, how much, how is it, what, why, etc)
*5. て as clause quoting mark (the pattern is too general)
*6. Katakana-ized ru-verb (バれる = good, バレる = not good, バレル = not good)
*7. ほど, ぐらい
*8. たい is always translated as first person (ex: 私たちも見たい = I want to see we)
*
*
*
*
*==============================================================================================================================
*to remove/replace names at the beginning
*since we used "Replace all names" method, we can't use normal way
*ex, we have a text from clipboard : アリス　「私の名前はアリスです、よろしくね」
*if we put only アリス, the アリス text inside the sentence will be removed too
*so put a unique condition like : (アリス　「)    <--- must use round braces (), otherwise it won't work
*(アリス　「)(ctrl-tab)「
*the result will be : 「私の名前はアリスです、よろしくね」
*that's it, so we don't have problem with "name at the beginning" anymore
*
*
*
*trying to remove any names at beginning (experimental)
*might break narations or multiple brackets texts. You might need to disable it on novel-text-mode game such as Fate, Tsukihime, Umineko etc.
*notes :
*to minimize text break you should only use one separator,
*mostly used is 「, while 『 is used for quote in jpn, and （ is used for "thought"
*not working when the game using multiple quote separator, please use name specific instead
*
*this is an example code for a game like Neko Koi (Whirlpool)
*where the text :
*- consist of speaker name, plus the name is repeatedly (ex: 美咲美咲美咲美咲)
*- when in dialogue mode the sentence separator is "「」"
*- when in thinking mode the sentence separator is "（）"
*- when in naration mode there is no separator, no speaker name
*- in dialogue, thinking, or naration mode, this game uses multiple type of quote separator
*obviously we can't use global name removal, it's impossible
*1. Firstly, remove speaker name for dialogue mode
*In this part, we can safely remove all names using (.+)
*read : gather any text until matching "「", then replace it with text contained in "slot position 5" which is "「"
*(^(【(.+)】|(.+))([「])){1}	$5
*2. Secondly, remove speaker name for thinking mode. Be careful to not mistook eng "(" with jap "（" symbol.
*In this part we have to put specific name, otherwise the text before a quote will be considered as a name too
*read : gather specific text until matching "（", then replace it with text contained in "slot position 9" which is "（"
*(美咲)\3+ means phrase repetition of 美咲,
*and \3 means text contained in "slot position 3" (see the order of "(", it is at 3th ), which is 美咲 too
*please be mind that max "save slot" is 9 (1-9)
*(^(司|(美咲)\3+|(真央)\4+|(ご先祖様)\5+|(陽南)\6+|(朔夜)\7+|(さやか)\8+|怜)(（))	$9
*
*how to remove unnecessary word inside a quote :
*sometimes there are situation like this :
*1. where font size and colour is included in text, like in Haramase series
*ex: 「私はアリス[c=255 s=20]です」
*2. or we got a kanji plus its furigana like in Zinmu (Alicesoft)
*ex: 「私の名前は緑[みどり]です」
*to remove those [c=255 s=20] or [みどり] :
*firstly, mark the separator (in this case with "z"), then remove anything inside "z"
*(\x5B)	z
*(\x5D)	z
*(z([^z]+)z)
*
*global name removal examples :
*be mind that those codes wouldn't handle a multilevel quotes text, 
*when this happen, just use ONLY ONE separator should fix it.
*1. pattern : name「dialogue」 or 【name】「dialogue」, separators : 「『（
*recommended, most games uses this pattern
*(^(【(.+)】|(.+))([「『（])){1}	$5
*(^(【(.+)】|(.+))([「])){1}	$5
*2. pattern : name　「dialogue」 or 【name】　「dialogue」, with a space before dialogue, separators : 「『（
*(^(【(.+)】|(.+))　([「『（])){1}	$5
*3. pattern : 「dialogue」name 
*known games uses this pattern: BaldrSky and any GIGA games, Shin Koihime Musou
*(([」』）])(【(.+)】|(.+))$)	$2
*(([」）])(【(.+)】|(.+))$)	$2
*4. pattern : [name]dialogue, separator : [ (square bracket)
*known games uses this pattern: G-Spot's Kyou no Okazu series and other "bruns engine" games
*notes :
*we can't put "[]" directly, because in regex it is an operator for grouping.
*so \x means specify a hex code of a character, 5B is "[" and 5D is "]"
*(^(\x5B(.+)\x5D)(.+))	「$4」
*
*how to replace a name :
*IMO changing name directly into English is bad. Because it could make a mistranslation.
*But it is needed if you are using other translation machine outside Atlas.
*these 3 codes are required, otherwise replacement won't work on when the name occured more than once in one text.
*1. This is for detecting name at the very beginning of text
*^ニナ	Nina
*2. This is for detecting name inside text
*(.)ニナ(.)	$1Nina$2
*3. This is for detecting name at the end of text
*二ナ$	Nina
*

*templates
*remove ・ when make a deep impression word
*(([あ-ん]{2,})・([あ-ん]{2,})・([あ-ん]{2,}))	$2x$3y$4
*(([あ-ん]{2,})・([あ-ん]{2,}))	$2z$3
*(([ア-ヴ]{2,})・([ア-ヴ]{2,})・([ア-ヴ]{2,}))	$2x$3y$4
*(([ア-ヴ]{2,})・([ア-ヴ]{2,}))	$2z$3
*(([一-龠]{2,})・([一-龠]{2,})・([一-龠]{2,}))	$2x$3y$4
*(([一-龠]{2,})・([一-龠]{2,}))	$2z$3
*(・)
*(([あ-ん]{2,})x([あ-ん]{2,})y([あ-ん]{2,}))	$2・$3・$4
*(([あ-ん]{2,})z([あ-ん]{2,}))	$2・$3
*(([ア-ヴ]{2,})x([ア-ヴ]{2,})y([ア-ヴ]{2,}))	$2・$3・$4
*(([ア-ヴ]{2,})z([ア-ヴ]{2,}))	$2・$3
*(([一-龠]{2,})x([一-龠]{2,})y([一-龠]{2,}))	$2・$3・$4
*(([一-龠]{2,})z([一-龠]{2,}))	$2・$3
*
*convert 「」 into 『』 in naration text
*this code is very useful on some games when uses different delimiter for quoting
*condition: speaker name must be removed!
*(^(「)(.+)([^」]$))	『$3$4
*(^([^「])(.+)([」]$))	$2$3』
*(^(「))	z
*((」)$)	y
*(「)	『
*(」)	』
*(^(z))	「
*((y)$)	」
*
*==============================================================================================================================
*now, let's try to cleaning sentences
*==============================================================================================================================
*1. Initial filter, removing useless symbols
*be careful, sometimes those symbols are required on specific games
*ex :
*- when between hiragana chars, sometimes ー or ― was used for replacing い or う
*- symbol like (・) used as firstname-lastname separator, while in other game used as … replacement
*
*remove jpn space (　) from sentence
*sometimes this occured on kirikiri engine based games
*how this happened? This is because there is a script inside kirikiri itself (ex: linebreak codes),
*and when agth get the text, it's considered as second line of text, but agth merge it in one line with (　) as a separator.
*Atlas don't have problem reading sentence even if there are (　), however in modifying text we need to remove it.
*disable it if you're not playing kirikiri games
*((.)　(.))	$2$3
*
*remove ・ when make a deep impression word
*disabled, try to see if LEC can handle it or not
*(([あ-ん]{2,})・([あ-ん]{2,})・([あ-ん]{2,}))	$2x$3y$4
*(([あ-ん]{2,})・([あ-ん]{2,}))	$2z$3
*(([ア-ヴ]{2,})・([ア-ヴ]{2,})・([ア-ヴ]{2,}))	$2x$3y$4
*(([ア-ヴ]{2,})・([ア-ヴ]{2,}))	$2z$3
*(([一-龠]{2,})・([一-龠]{2,})・([一-龠]{2,}))	$2x$3y$4
*(([一-龠]{2,})・([一-龠]{2,}))	$2z$3
*(・)
*(([あ-ん]{2,})x([あ-ん]{2,})y([あ-ん]{2,}))	$2・$3・$4
*(([あ-ん]{2,})z([あ-ん]{2,}))	$2・$3
*(([ア-ヴ]{2,})x([ア-ヴ]{2,})y([ア-ヴ]{2,}))	$2・$3・$4
*(([ア-ヴ]{2,})z([ア-ヴ]{2,}))	$2・$3
*(([一-龠]{2,})x([一-龠]{2,})y([一-龠]{2,}))	$2・$3・$4
*(([一-龠]{2,})z([一-龠]{2,}))	$2・$3

*symbols replacements :
*\x21 = hex code for "?", \x3F = hex code for "!"
*replacing this is important, I forgot why I disabled it...
\x21	！
\x3F	？

*！？	？
(([０-９])(・)([０-９]))	$2─$4
*how to detect ・ whether it's a name-separator or sentence-separator safely?
*(([^・]{2,})(・)([^・]{2,}))	$2　$4
*
(([０-９])([－―─])([Ａ-Ｚ０-９]))	$2x$4
(－|―|─|[・]{2,}|[･]{2,}|･･･|・・・|‥)	…
(([０-９])x([Ａ-Ｚ０-９]))	$2─$3
*LEC, temporary disabled "・"
*(・)
*symbols like ≪《＜≫》＞ maybe better use on game specific code only
*([≪《])	＜
*([≫》])	＞
*a symbol like ☆ is a little complicated
*sometimes used as :
*1. separator between words (らき☆すた) => (らき　すた)
*2. punctuation (えへへ☆) => (えへへ。)
*how to properly detect it I'm still blank...
(([あ-ん])☆([あ-ん]))	$2　$3
*♪ already handled by VNR
*masking symbols, try with … instead of 。
*first limit to 1 symbols
([★☆♪❤])\1+	$1
♪	」MS0001「
★	」MS0002「
☆	」MS0003「
❤	」MS0004「
*(★|☆)	。

*remove "（？）", dunno what does this  means, but I often see this...
(([一-龠あ-んア-ヴ])(（？）)([一-龠あ-んア-ヴ]))	$2$4

*-------------------------------------------------
*if there is a symbol repetition (ex : ーーーーーー, ああああああ), we replace it with just once
*we can't remove it entirely because it's sometimes used on western terms.
*can be used to remove hiragana & katakana vowel repetitions too
*
(([～ーっッァィゥェォんンを])\2+)	$2
*
*exception
((あ){2,}(の)([っ、。？！…」』）]))	$2$3$4
*
((ア){2,})	$2$2
((ウ){2,})	$2$2
((エ){2,})	$2$2
((オ){2,})	$2$2
((あ){2,})	$2$2
((う){2,})	$2$2
((え){2,})	$2$2
((お){2,})	$2$2
*save word いい because it has a meaning
*but don't group い with イ, because will break text like 面白いイベント
((い){3,})	$2$2$2
((イ){2,})	$2$2

*
*put pre-mod lines here :
*
*firstly limit any repeating small vowels to 1, for next process
(([ぁぃぅぇぉ])\2+)	$2
*---しませぇぇぇん---
(([けげせぜてでへべめれぺ])([ぇ]+)([んン])([っ、。？！…）」』]))	$2$4$5
*remove any text after small vowels (ex: あぁああ)
*katakana is disabled, might break text like ガーディアン, we gonna need better pattern.
(([ぁぃぅぇぉァィゥェォ])([っぁぃぅぇぉァィゥェォあいうえおアイウエオ]{2,})([んン])([、。？！…）」』]))	$5
*(([ぁぃぅぇぉァィゥェォ])([っぁぃぅぇぉァィゥェォあいうえおアイウエオんン]{2,})([、。？！…）」』]))	$4

*
*kawainaatteomotta, remove the "naa"
*I found that なぁと思 can be translated by Atlas
*however なぁって思 is not
*maybe because って is a (coll), that's why it'll break translation
*note: 
*んじゃないか + なぁと思 = ok
*のじゃないか + なぁと思 = ok (however, the meaning will different)
*んじゃないか + と思 = broken <-- this is our big problem
*のじゃないか + と思 = ok
*there is still one problem, the translation is a negative state-of-being :
*いいんじゃないかなぁと思った = It was thought that it wasn't nice
*what we expect is = It was thought whether it is nice or not (confirmation)
*problem lies in かなぁと
*かなぁと = the first clause is translated as negative state-of-being
*かと = the first clause is translated as probably/confirmation
*
*save
((んじゃないか)(な[あぁ]と)([思想]|おも))	$2$3x$4
((んじゃないか)(なって)([思想]|おも))	$2$3x$4
((んじゃないか)(な[あぁ]って)([思想]|おも))	$2$3x$4

*--- handling partial adverbal/onomatopoeic ---
*ex: 「にぱー、と彼女は笑い」
*Atlas translation : "[Nipa-], She smiles solving"
*"solving" exist because there is "と" coming from partial にぱーと (adv)
*how to handle that separated text :
*1. by joining it, this way gives better translation, however without a good detection method it's kinda very unsafe
*2. by removing "と", so the translation clear enough to understand --> "[Nipa-], She smiles"
*removing と at the beginning sentence, to avoid "solve" translation from Atlas
*hiragana part seems inaccurate, but I'll include it anyway
*also this code might break "join by onomatopoeic" code later...
*join directly
*alright, time to deal with it. Put any partial onomatopeic here

*==============================================================================================================================
*2. Cleaning up partial chars on text. (Sequence order is : middle --> beginning --> end)
*I decided to remove those chars because a "はー、はー、はー" doesn't always means a moaning or panting sfx
*it might not working on text with only partial chars like : 「は、は、は、は！　あー」
*but we can let TA's substitution handle it.
*only removing ONE character, otherwise there is a possibility to accidently that a jpn word consist in two or more characters got removed too.
*
*Note: some word like ね will be gone too, however it's no problem since you'll never know how to detect whether it means "hey" or "right"
*
*2.1. Removing partial characters at middle sentences (mostly in h-scene)
*a search including a round dots (。) is tricky. The character is ignored if it's on the beginning of a line, but of course in practise there is no way a sentence will firstly started by (。)
*so don't bother if it looks wrong, because it's working actually.
*pattern = 、あ、 or 、あ… or 。あ、 or 。あ… or …あ、 or …あ… or 。　あ、 or 。　あ… or 、　あ、 or 、　あ… or …　あ、 or …　あ…
*or 、あー、 or 、あー… or 。あー、 or 。あー… or …あー、 or …あー… or 。　あー、 or 。　あー… or 、　あー、 or 、　あー… or …　あー、
*or …　あー… (replace with left side char)
((、|。|…|。　|、　|…　)([あ-ん]|[ア-ヴ]|(([あ-ん]|[ア-ヴ])ー))(、|…))+	$2
*pattern = ！あ、 or ！あ。 or ！あ… or ？あ、 or ？あ。 or ？あ… or ！　あ、 or ！　あ… or ？　あ、 or ？　あ…
*or ！あー、 or ！あー。 or ！あー… or ？あー、 or ？あー。 or ？あー… or ！　あー、 or ！　あー… or ？　あー、 or ？　あー… (replace with left side char)
((！|？|　)([あ-ん]|[ア-ヴ]|(([あ-ん]|[ア-ヴ])ー))(、|。|…|？|！))+	$2
*pattern = …あ。 or …あ！ or …あ？ or 、あ。 or 、あ！ or 、あ？
*or …あー。 or …あー！ or …あー？ or 、あー。 or 、あー！ or 、あー？ (replace with right side char)
((…|、)([あ-ん]|[ア-ヴ]|(([あ-ん]|[ア-ヴ])ー))(。|！|？))+	$6

*
*===========================================
*handling kansai/osaka-ben etc
*notes :
*hard to do :
*1. はる = polite "to-do", it's hard to detect verb + はる using regex
*2. reversing って, in kansai-ben "っ" is not used, instead the word is shortened (ex: 思って become 思て, 言ったら become 言うたら)
*3. や = だ. But since や means "and", so we can't replace any や with だ
*4. やる = する, this should be no problem, however it'll collide with や for plain copula. (ex: やって -> だって for no.3 isn't good for no. 4)
*5. やろ = confirmation form, we could replace it with another (exp), but (again) be mind that やろ could means やる (to do)
*6. ちゃう = じゃない, must be careful to not screw てしまう meaning
*7. っちゅ = not just a plain って (read --- って --- section for detail)
*8. はよ、よう、and another simple (adj)/(adv) words
*9. ksb + delinquent talks = nice combo, complicated...
*currently, the best method to handle it is to put each specific words into dictionary, it's gonna be a big work!
*
*save
((も)(かまへん)([、。…？！」』）]))	$2x$4
*

*
*--- とる ---
*おる -> いる
*とる -> ている, or just て for -te form
*general pattern is verb + とる
*ex: 
*1. past form, ex: 聞いた become 聞いとった
*2. present form, ex: 使う become 使こうとる
*first try, let's see if we can replace it without checking the verb type
*if failed, we must handle it specifically
*とった	-->た
*っとった	-->った
*
*save
(([一-龠])(とっても))	$2x$3
((奪)(いとる))	$2x$3
(([をがにへとでのはも])と(る)([をがにへとでのはも])([、。…？！」』）]))	$2t$3$4$5

*
*--- Kanji + っといて ---
*ex: 撮っといて
*not related with ksb, but I put here to make it easy to find
*this word could means :
*1. -te form
*2. -te form + おく, because といて => とく => で/て+おく
*however we can't use general pattern, because a -te form could ended by て or (ん)で
*misplacing that て or (ん)で will break translation.
*as a test, let's trying to use general pattern

*---handling archaic & elder dialect---

*and be careful to not breaking じゃ from (col) of でしまう

*
*======================================================================================
*---どう---
*in order to make a proper "questioning" form by どう, 
*we have to replace incorrect (exp) or "question mark (？)"
*note: don't confusedly mixing plain copula (だ、です、だろう、でしょう) with to-do (する、しよう、でしよう)
*when following たら, どうでしょう is not the same as どうでしよう
*ですか or just か gives different translation, however the meaning still the same way
*は +　どう  + ですか = how about (note: たら can't joined with は)
*たら + どう = why don't (note: mustn't ended by "？")
*たら + どうか = another alternative translation
*
*jyanai + たら + どう will result error (じゃなかった or らではなかったら)
(じゃな|ではな)(かったらどう)([、。？！…」』）])	$1$2する$3
*
*たら + どう + だ、だい、だろう = not working
*たら + どう + でしょう = working, but IMO better using どう。
((たら|んだら)(どう)(だ|だい|だろう|だろ|でしょ|でしょう|です)か([、。？！…」』）]))	$2$3。$5
((たら|んだら)(どう)(だ|だい|だろう|だろ|でしょ|でしょう|です)([のか、。？！…」』）]))	$2$3$5
((たら|んだら)(どう)？)	$2$3。
((たら|んだら)(どう)(かな|かしら)([、。？！…」』）]))	$2$3。$5
*
*(obj-prt) + どう + だ、だい = not working
*(obj-prt) + どう + だろう = working, but must be ended by か or ？
*(obj-prt) + どう + でしょう = working
*(([はが])(どう)(だ|だい|だろう|だろ|でしょ|でしょう|です)か([、。？！…」』）]))	$2$3。$5
(([はが])(どう)(だ|だい|だろう|だろ|でしょ)([のか、。？！…」』）]))	$2$3でしょう$5
(([はが])(どう)([、。？！…」』）]))	$2$3ですか$4
*note: when as clause, the translation still not good enough

*save

*
*---main code---
*I've tried with comma and か, now trying with ですか
*the reason I changed darou/deshou into desuka is because sentence ended by just darou/deshou is ambiguous
*moreover, "might" translation is kinda have a special pattern in Atlas
*if the sentence is incorrect then translation will screwed.
*if you still want the original darou/deshou translation, just disable this part
*disabled partial, LEC
*let's see if LEC can handle deshou & darou or not
*だろ & でしょ = だ
*だろう & でしょう = will be (polite version?)
*困るだろ = can't be translated
*困るだろう = good, 困るでしょ = good, 困るでしょう = good
*
*handling repetition

*-te form + た = "did" + verb-s

*
*---っか---
*verb + っか should be translated into "let's", not a volitional, or a probably
*ろっか when changed into ろうか, the confirmation form is gone
*ex: 
*帰ろっか when replaced with 帰ろうか
*expected translation : "Shall we return?"
*current translation : "Let's return"
*the problem is because 帰る is u-verb, 
*so the proper one should be 帰りましょうか
*however, because we don't have subject here, Atlas will translate it as "Shall I return?"
*logically ろっか only means polite volitional form
*there should be no word like 消えろっか, well... if that's really happened we need to change the code...
((ろ)っ(か)([、。？！…」』）]))	りましょう$3$4
(([れみ])っ(か)([、。？！…」』）]))	$2ましょう$3$4

*--- その ---

*
*---かな---
*かな means "I wonder", but in Atlas we can't do anything with it.
*the proper word type is particle-preposition (not noun), but somehow Atlas can't recognize it
*so there are 2 ways to handle this :
*1. Convert it into a statement form by breaking かな and replace it directly with english "I wonder"
*2. Convert it into a questioning form by treating か as question (prt) + な as (exp), which な in here can be removed
*
((たら|ない)(かな)([。、？！…）」』]))	$2x$4
(([^。、？！…「『（])(か)な([。、？！…）」』]))	$2$3$4
((たら|ない)(x)([。、？！…）」』]))	$2かな$4
*
*---かしら---
*かしら is another "I wonder" too, it has the same problem as かな
((どうしようか)しら([。、？！…）」』]))	$2$3

((か)しら([。、？！…）」』]))	$2$3

*
*---じゃない---
*sentence ended by じゃない is ambiguous
*ex: 「あら？アリスちゃんじゃない」
*literal (Atlas) translation : "It's not Alice" --- negative state-of-being
*interpretative translation : "Isn't it Alice?" --- confirmation, notice the translation become a question even the original doesn't
*while the first translation is correct (by grammar), but we expecting the second translation.
*you will find this "confusing" sentence often
*
*if "janai" followed by "darou" or "deshou", "ja" must be replaced with "deha"
*replace "darou" with "deshou", because "deshou" have less problem than "darou"
*after "deshou", whether followed by "ka" or punctuation, it doesn't matter
*
*words not yet solved:
*つもりじゃない？ --- need to solve つもり first
*
*pre-mod
*LEC can't handle いいじゃんいいじゃん, make it 1x
((いいじゃん)\2([、。？！…」』）]))	$2$3

*--- 目指す ---

*
*--- いざ ---
*いざ already have an internal translation, mean "now"
*however, it doesn't always properly translated
*but if we register it as "now" (adv), it'll translated good enough
*but, it'll break phrase related with いざ
*ex: いざなって (invite)
*so let's replace that hiragana into kanji
((いざなって))	誘って

*selfnotes : しゃいじゃった
*
*--- ちゃ ---
*ちゃ pattern :
*ちゃ + (adj) = replace with ては
*ちゃ + う = no problem, Atlas can translate it
*
*to fix ちゃ, there're two possibilites :
*ちゃう (unintentionally) or ては (conditionally)
*or a partial word came from a (suf) like ちゃん, but we'll ignore it
*normally a (conditionally) text is ended by (、) or (…), but in some case it isn't...
*pre-save
((なく)っちゃ([。？！」』）]))	$2ては$3
(([、。？！…「『（])(お兄|おにい|おねえ|[一-龠]+)(ちゃ|ちゃあん|ちゃああん)([、。？！…」』）]))	$2$3ちゃん$5
*save
*((めちゃめ|むちゃく|いちゃい|ぴちゃぴ|むちゃく)ちゃ([、。？！…」』）]))	$2x$3

*
*---te form---
*(first priority is te form, followed by masu stem, so it wouldn't break word like 甘えて)
*when -te form meets ちゃ, then only one て is used, ex: 顔をしてちゃダメ --> 顔をしてはダメ, not 顔をしててはダメ
*selfnotes: ちゃえ(ば) should be no probs, for the moment...
(([^、。？！…「『（])([っせべげけめねれて来きしくういえ]|[さわばがかまならあた][れせ]|しえ|なく|まし|[あえ来こ](られ|させ)|あっ)(て)ちゃ([、。？！…」』）]))	$2$3$5は$6
(([^、。？！…「『（])([っせべげけめねれて来きしくういえ]|[さわばがかまならあた][れせ]|しえ|なく|まし|[あえ来こ](られ|させ)|あっ)(て)(ちゃ)(いい|だめ|らめ|いけない|まずい|良い|駄目|ダメ|イイ|いられない|いけません|いけない))	$2$3$5は$7
(([^、。？！…「『（])([っせべげけめねれて来きしくういえ]|[さわばがかまならあた][れせ]|しえ|なく|まし|[あえ来こ](られ|させ)|あっ)(て)(ちゃ)([^っういえおわん]))	$2$3$5は$7
*
*---masu stem---
*handling ちゃ in the middle of text is hard
*here's the step :
*firstly read if word before ちゃ is a masu stem、this is the hard part...
*check what's after ちゃ :
*if う then it's a unintentionally form
*if not う, it should be replaced with ては
*and don't forget to be carefull with (adv) and (noun) too
*btw, if you're lazy, you can add ちゃ as prt-preposition in Atlas (ex: then)
*ex: 待たせちゃ駄目, the translation will be like :
*ちゃ as prt-preposition : It waits and it is not good then
*ちゃ as ては : It is not good when waiting
(なっ)ちゃ(た)	$1て$2
(([^、。？！…「『（])([っせべげけめねれて来きしくういえ]|[さわばがかまならあた][れせ]|しえ|なく|まし|[あえ来こ](られ|させ)|あっ)(ちゃ)(いい|だめ|らめ|いけない|まずい|良い|駄目|ダメ|イイ|いられない|いけません|いけない))	$2$3ては$6
(([^、。？！…「『（])([っせべげけめねれて来きしくういえ]|[さわばがかまならあた][れせ]|しえ|なく|まし|[あえ来こ](られ|させ)|あっ)(ちゃ)([^っういえおわんま]))	$2$3ては$6
(([^、。？！…「『（])(ぎ)(ちゃ)([^っういえおわん]))	$2$3ては$5
((にな)(ちゃ)([^っういえおわ]))	$2ては$4
((にな|[一-龠])(ちゃ)(いい|だめ|らめ|いけない|まずい|良い|駄目|ダメ|イイ|失礼))	$2ては$4

*try to fix ちゃん after ては, will be removed if not working
(ては(あん)([、。？！…」』）]))	ちゃん$3

*restore

*
*-te form + らした ---
*causative past form, but instead of masu stem, -te form is used.
*ex: 
*見てらした -> 見させた
*言ってらした -> 言わせた
*however, it'll be difficult to change it. Especially verb ended by んで and って
*
*1. して + らした -> させた (-す)
*2.1. いて + らした -> かせた (-く)
*2.2. いで + らした -> がせた (-ぐ)
*3.1. んで + らした -> ませた　(-む)
*3.2. んで + らした -> ばせた　(-ぶ)
*3.3. んで + らした -> なせた　(-ぬ)
*4.1. って + らした -> らせた　(-る)
*4.2. って + らした -> わせた　(-う)
*4.3. って + らした -> たせた　(-つ)
*5. きて + らした -> こさせた (-くる)
*6. 行って + らした -> 行かせた (-行く)
*
(([一-龠])(して)(らした))	$2させた
(([一-龠])(いて)(らした))	$2かせた
(([一-龠])(いで)(らした))	$2がせた
(([一-龠])(て)(らした))	$2させた
((行って)(らした))	行かせた
((きて)(らした))	こさせた
*って and んで gonna need specific replacement in TA dictionary
*refer to no 3 and 4 above for correct conjugation
*
*-te form + られる ---
*passive form, but instead of masu stem, -te form is used
(([一-龠])(して)ら(れる|れない))	$2さ$4

*--- classical (adj) + ござる or 出でる/いでる ---
*pattern :
*1. あ row (早い --> 早う)
*2. い row (大きい --> 大きゅう)
*3. う row (安い --> 安う)
*4. お row (面白い --> 面白う)
*selfnotes: impossible to fix, just create as new word in Atlas

*お早うございます = good morning

*
*--- って ---
*って is another confusion, it means :
*1. (coll) of という or というの or というのは
*2. (coll) of と言って(も)
*3. (coll) of として(も)
*4. と
*5. といって
*Generally it's kinda a replacement of quoting particle, in english it should be like a "It is said that..."
*
*sentence ended by なって is hard too, because it means :
*1. な from negative imperative form
*2. な from suffix
*3. な from なる (become)
*4. a part of a -te form verb conjugation
*
*save

*
*--- て + an (adj) clause ---
*still not sure how to handle this
*the focus meaning will be different
*ex: 警備システムを戻しては良い
*with は, the focus is the (adj) clause
*without は, the focus is first clause
*there are three possibilities here :
*1. -te form + (adj) clause <-- need fix with は
*2. masu stem + たって (tatte here means "even") + (adj) clause <-- no need fix
*3. past form + って (coll) + (adj) clause <-- need fix with といって
*how to properly detect it?
*
*save past form
*selfnotes: past form like った don't need a fix, however there is still a possibility a -te form...
*((ったって|そして)(良[いか]|いい))	$2x$3
*
*(([っせべげけめねれて来きしくういえ]|[さわばがかまならあた][れせ]|しえ|なく|まし|[あえ来こ](られ|させ)|あっ)(て)(良[いか]))	$2$4は$5
*(([っせべげけめねれて来きしくういえ]|[さわばがかまならあた][れせ]|しえ|なく|まし|[あえ来こ](られ|させ)|あっ)(て)(いい))	$2$4は良い
*restore
*((ったって|そして)x(良[いか]|いい))	$2$3

*5. Lastly, finalize script.
*LEC
*a sentence ended with question mark "？" always translated along with the next sentence
*therefore we need to separate it with "。"
*([？])([^。！」])	$1。$2
*replacing quotes so can be translated by LEC
*[《『]	“
*[》』]	”
*removing open brackets "「" because LEC can't accept it
*disabled : VNR already handled it
*([「])
*handling "…" based on some pattern
*revert masked symbols
[。」]MS0001「	♪
[。」]MS0002「	★
[。」]MS0003「	☆
[。」]MS0004「	❤
*clean up again, limit to 1
([★☆♪❤])\1+	$1
*"…" could act as separator like "。" or as comma "、"
…+(？)	$1
…+(」)	。$1
*for some reason "…+" is skipped by VNR, so we'll apply this rule inside VNR instead
*…+	。
*removing close brackets "」" because LEC can't accept it
*disabled : VNR already handled it
*([！？])[」]	$1
*([^！？])[」]	$1。
